<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Повестка</span> <span class="kw kw-o">заседания</span> нашего Совета <span class="kw kw-y">отражает</span>

几乎<span class="kw kw-y">整个</span>文化领域的多<span class="kw kw-g">样性</span>。特别是，我们<span class="kw kw-c">必须</span>考虑与电影制<span class="kw kw-b">作相</span>关的问题
和电<span class="kw kw-v">影发</span>行。</p>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 В <span class="kw kw-r">последние</span> годы немало <span class="kw kw-o">сделано</span> для
того, <span class="kw kw-y">чтобы</span> обеспечить интенсивное <span class="kw kw-g">развитие</span> национальной киноиндустрии,
<span class="kw kw-c">повысить</span> её конкурентоспособность. <span class="kw kw-b">Вместе</span> с тем необходимо <span class="kw kw-v">обеспечить</span>
знакомство, прежде <span class="kw kw-r">всего</span> нашей молодёжи, и с <span class="kw kw-o">более</span> ранними, лучшими <span class="kw kw-y">образцами</span>
отечественного кино, с <span class="kw kw-g">его</span> давней, славной <span class="kw kw-c">историей</span>.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 In <span class="kw kw-r">recent</span> <span class="kw kw-o">years</span>, <span class="kw kw-y">much</span> <span class="kw kw-g">has</span> <span class="kw kw-c">been</span> <span class="kw kw-b">done</span> to
in order to ensure <span class="kw kw-v">intensive</span> development of the national film <span class="kw kw-r">industry</span>,
increase its competitiveness. <span class="kw kw-o">At</span> the same time, it is <span class="kw kw-y">necessary</span> to ensure
acquaintance, first of <span class="kw kw-g">all</span>, with our youth, and with earlier, <span class="kw kw-c">better</span> examples
Russian cinema, with <span class="kw kw-b">its</span> long, glorious history.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">近年</span>来，我们<span class="kw kw-o">做了</span>很多工作
<span class="kw kw-y">为保</span>障民族电<span class="kw kw-g">影产</span>业集约发<span class="kw kw-c">展</span>，
提高其竞<span class="kw kw-b">争力</span>。同时，需要<span class="kw kw-v">保证</span>
首先，熟悉<span class="kw kw-r">我们</span>的青年时<span class="kw kw-o">代</span>，以及更早、<span class="kw kw-y">更好</span>的例子
<span class="kw kw-g">俄罗</span>斯电影有<span class="kw kw-c">着悠</span>久而辉煌的历史。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 В <span class="kw kw-r">целом</span> следует более <span class="kw kw-o">глубоко</span> и системно рассказывать <span class="kw kw-y">детям</span>, подросткам, молодёжи <span class="kw kw-g">вообще</span> о вкладе российского

<span class="kw kw-r">важный</span> элемент воспитания.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 In <span class="kw kw-r">general</span>, <span class="kw kw-o">children</span>, <span class="kw kw-y">adolescents</span>, and young <span class="kw kw-g">people</span> in general should be told <span class="kw kw-c">more</span> deeply and systematically about the <span class="kw kw-b">contribution</span> of the Russian
art, our <span class="kw kw-v">great</span> masters of different eras <span class="kw kw-r">into</span> world culture. This is <span class="kw kw-o">very</span>

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">总的</span><span class="kw kw-o">来说</span>，<span class="kw kw-y">应该</span>更深<span class="kw kw-g">入</span>、更系统地向儿<span class="kw kw-c">童</span>、青少年和年轻<span class="kw kw-b">人讲</span>述俄罗斯的贡<span class="kw kw-v">献</span>。
艺术，把我们不<span class="kw kw-r">同时</span>代的大师融入<span class="kw kw-o">到世</span>界文化中。这是<span class="kw kw-y">非常</span>
教育的一个重<span class="kw kw-g">要组</span>成部分。</p>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">При</span> <span class="kw kw-o">этом</span>, <span class="kw kw-y">уверен</span>, <span class="kw kw-g">подрастающие</span>
<span class="kw kw-c">поколения</span> должны не только знать <span class="kw kw-b">искусство</span>, но и, что называется, иметь
возможность <span class="kw kw-v">его</span> практиковать. С ранних лет <span class="kw kw-r">обучаться</span> живописи и танцу, музыке.
У <span class="kw kw-o">нас</span> в стране выстроена блестящая <span class="kw kw-y">многоуровневая</span> система такого образования, и <span class="kw kw-g">она</span> нуждается в постоянной поддержке.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">At</span> the <span class="kw kw-o">same</span> <span class="kw kw-y">time</span>, I am <span class="kw kw-g">sure</span> that growing up
<span class="kw kw-c">generations</span> should not only <span class="kw kw-b">know</span> art, but also, <span class="kw kw-v">as</span> they say, have
<span class="kw kw-r">opportunity</span> to practice it. From an <span class="kw kw-o">early</span> age, learn painting, <span class="kw kw-y">dance</span>, and music.
Our country <span class="kw kw-g">has</span> built a brilliant multi-level <span class="kw kw-c">system</span> of such education, and it <span class="kw kw-b">needs</span> constant support.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">同时</span>我也确信，<span class="kw kw-o">在成</span>长过程中
<span class="kw kw-y">几代</span>人不仅应<span class="kw kw-g">该了</span>解艺术，<span class="kw kw-c">而且</span>正如他们<span class="kw kw-b">所说</span>，
有机会练<span class="kw kw-v">习一</span>下。从小<span class="kw kw-r">就学</span>习绘画、<span class="kw kw-o">舞蹈</span>和音乐。
<span class="kw kw-y">我国</span>已经建立<span class="kw kw-g">了完</span>善的多层次的教育体系，需要不断的支持。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 На <span class="kw kw-r">прошлом</span> <span class="kw kw-o">заседании</span> мы говорили о <span class="kw kw-y">задачах</span>

<span class="kw kw-v">Федерации</span>.</p>

infrastructural <span class="kw kw-y">development</span> of the cultural sector. In this <span class="kw kw-g">regard</span>, I would like to draw <span class="kw kw-c">attention</span> to the need to strengthen work in <span class="kw kw-b">this</span> area in the regions of the Russian <span class="kw kw-v">Federation</span>.
Federation.</p>

<span class="kw kw-y">文化</span>产业基础<span class="kw kw-g">设施</span>建设。在这<span class="kw kw-c">方面</span>，我谨提请<span class="kw kw-b">注意</span>俄罗斯联<span class="kw kw-v">邦各</span>地区加强<span class="kw kw-r">这一</span>领域工作的必要性。
联邦。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Прошу</span> <span class="kw kw-o">активнее</span> <span class="kw kw-y">обеспечивать</span> модернизацию и <span class="kw kw-g">строительство</span>
новых учреждений культуры, <span class="kw kw-c">их</span> оснащение, содействовать творческим <span class="kw kw-b">деятелям</span> и объединениям в части предоставления <span class="kw kw-v">льготных</span> условий аренды помещений и <span class="kw kw-r">территорий</span>.
Прежде всего такую <span class="kw kw-o">помощь</span> следует оказывать тем, <span class="kw kw-y">кто</span> занимается с молодыми
людьми, с <span class="kw kw-g">молодёжью</span>.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 I <span class="kw kw-r">ask</span> <span class="kw kw-o">you</span> to <span class="kw kw-y">more</span> <span class="kw kw-g">actively</span> <span class="kw kw-c">ensure</span> <span class="kw kw-b">modernization</span> and construction
new <span class="kw kw-v">cultural</span> institutions, their equipment, <span class="kw kw-r">assist</span> artists and associations in terms of <span class="kw kw-o">providing</span> preferential terms for renting <span class="kw kw-y">premises</span> and territories.
First of all, <span class="kw kw-g">such</span> assistance should be provided to <span class="kw kw-c">those</span> who work with young <span class="kw kw-b">people</span>.
people, with young people.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">请你</span>们更加积<span class="kw kw-o">极地</span>搞好现代<span class="kw kw-y">化建</span>设
新的<span class="kw kw-g">文化</span>机构及其<span class="kw kw-c">设备</span>协助艺术<span class="kw kw-b">家和</span>协会提供<span class="kw kw-v">租用</span>场地和领<span class="kw kw-r">土的</span>优惠条件。
<span class="kw kw-o">首先</span>，应该向那<span class="kw kw-y">些从</span>事青年工<span class="kw kw-g">作的</span>人提供这种帮助。
人们，和年轻人。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Очень</span> важно поддерживать тех, <span class="kw kw-o">кто</span>
пишет книги, пьесы, <span class="kw kw-y">киносценарии</span>, стихи для детей, <span class="kw kw-g">молодёжи</span>, не забывая, как
говорил уже <span class="kw kw-c">известный</span> детский классик, «сегодня – <span class="kw kw-b">дети</span>, а завтра – народ».</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">It</span> is <span class="kw kw-o">very</span> <span class="kw kw-y">important</span> to support <span class="kw kw-g">those</span> who
writes books, <span class="kw kw-c">plays</span>, film scripts, poems for <span class="kw kw-b">children</span>, youth, not forgetting <span class="kw kw-v">how</span>
the well-known children&#x27;s <span class="kw kw-r">classic</span> said, “today are children, and <span class="kw kw-o">tomorrow</span> are people.”</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">支持</span><span class="kw kw-o">那些</span>人非常重<span class="kw kw-y">要</span>
为儿童、青少<span class="kw kw-g">年写</span>书、戏剧、电影<span class="kw kw-c">剧本</span>、诗歌，不要忘记<span class="kw kw-b">如何</span>
著名的儿童经<span class="kw kw-v">典说</span>：“今天是孩子，<span class="kw kw-r">明天</span>是人”。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Вообще</span> в <span class="kw kw-o">Год</span> <span class="kw kw-y">единства</span> народов <span class="kw kw-g">России</span>
необходимо обратить больше <span class="kw kw-c">внимания</span> на литературу и книжную отрасль, <span class="kw kw-b">особенно</span> в регионах, на авторов и переводчиков, <span class="kw kw-v">пишущих</span> на национальных языках, но включённых в <span class="kw kw-r">общее</span> российское единое литературное <span class="kw kw-o">пространство</span>.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 In <span class="kw kw-r">general</span>, in the <span class="kw kw-o">Year</span> of Unity of the Peoples of <span class="kw kw-y">Russia</span>
it is necessary to pay <span class="kw kw-g">more</span> attention to literature and the book <span class="kw kw-c">industry</span>, especially in the regions, to authors and <span class="kw kw-b">translators</span> who write in national <span class="kw kw-v">languages</span>, but are included in the general <span class="kw kw-r">Russian</span> unified literary space.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">总的</span><span class="kw kw-o">来说</span>，在俄罗斯<span class="kw kw-y">人民</span>团结年
有必<span class="kw kw-g">要更</span>多地关注文学<span class="kw kw-c">和图</span>书业，特别是在<span class="kw kw-b">各地</span>区，关注以民<span class="kw kw-v">族语</span>言写作但被纳<span class="kw kw-r">入俄</span>罗斯统一文学<span class="kw kw-o">空间</span>的作家和翻译<span class="kw kw-y">家</span>。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Давайте</span> <span class="kw kw-o">перейдём</span> к нашей работе, к <span class="kw kw-y">повестке</span>. Слово Владимиру Ростиславовичу
<span class="kw kw-g">Мединскому</span>. Пожалуйста, Владимир Ростиславович.</p>

<span class="kw kw-c">territories</span>, it is carried <span class="kw kw-b">out</span> by all <span class="kw kw-v">departments</span>. Question about <span class="kw kw-r">restoration</span>

<span class="kw kw-g">regions</span> through the joint <span class="kw kw-c">efforts</span> of regional governments, <span class="kw kw-b">VOOPIK</span> [All-Russian

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">边境</span>和新历史<span class="kw kw-o">地区</span>的文化历<span class="kw kw-y">史古</span>迹的记录<span class="kw kw-g">和保</span>护工作已<span class="kw kw-c">经开</span>始。

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 В <span class="kw kw-r">то</span> же время на <span class="kw kw-o">территории</span> ДНР и ЛНР по <span class="kw kw-y">Вашему</span> поручению уже <span class="kw kw-g">восстановлены</span> крупные мемориальные

<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">At</span> the same time, on the <span class="kw kw-o">territory</span> of the DPR and LPR, on <span class="kw kw-y">your</span> instructions, large <span class="kw kw-g">memorials</span> have already <span class="kw kw-c">been</span> restored

fascism &quot;<span class="kw kw-o">Mine</span> 4/4-bis&quot;, the <span class="kw kw-y">memorial</span> complex of military <span class="kw kw-g">glory</span> on the Mius River - <span class="kw kw-c">there</span>,
where the so-called <span class="kw kw-b">insurmountable</span> German defense “<span class="kw kw-v">Eastern</span> Wall” took <span class="kw kw-r">place</span>,
memorial complex “<span class="kw kw-o">Sharp</span> Grave”, “Prince <span class="kw kw-y">Igor</span>” - all this was

The work was carried out over the past two years.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">与此</span>同时，根据<span class="kw kw-o">您的</span>指示，在朝<span class="kw kw-y">鲜民</span>主主义人<span class="kw kw-g">民共</span>和国和人<span class="kw kw-c">民共</span>和国境内，<span class="kw kw-b">大型</span>纪念馆已<span class="kw kw-v">经恢</span>复

法西<span class="kw kw-g">斯主</span>义“Mine 4/4-bis”，米乌<span class="kw kw-c">斯河</span>上的军事<span class="kw kw-b">荣耀</span>纪念馆 - <span class="kw kw-v">在那</span>里，
所谓<span class="kw kw-r">不可</span>逾越的德<span class="kw kw-o">国防</span>御“东墙”<span class="kw kw-y">发生</span>的地方，
<span class="kw kw-g">纪念</span>馆“尖锐<span class="kw kw-c">的坟</span>墓”，“伊戈<span class="kw kw-b">尔王</span>子” - 所有<span class="kw kw-v">这些</span>都是
被乌<span class="kw kw-r">克兰</span>武装部队<span class="kw kw-o">轰炸</span>的，以及“不败者”青年近卫军纪念馆。
这项工作是在过去两年里进行的。</p>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 За <span class="kw kw-r">последние</span> <span class="kw kw-o">десять</span> лет
открыто <span class="kw kw-y">более</span> полутора тысяч новых <span class="kw kw-g">кинозалов</span> по всей стране. Каждый <span class="kw kw-c">год</span> мы

из них – молодёжь и <span class="kw kw-r">дети</span>. Планируется к 2030 году <span class="kw kw-o">открыть</span> ещё 900 киноцентров,
<span class="kw kw-y">кинозалов</span>. Мне кажется, что это важнейшая <span class="kw kw-g">вообще</span> задача, которая выполняется
<span class="kw kw-c">Правительством</span>, Министерством культуры.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">Over</span> the past ten <span class="kw kw-o">years</span>
More than <span class="kw kw-y">one</span> and a half thousand <span class="kw kw-g">new</span> cinema halls <span class="kw kw-c">have</span> been opened <span class="kw kw-b">throughout</span> the country. Every <span class="kw kw-v">year</span> we
we <span class="kw kw-r">get</span> an increase in the number of <span class="kw kw-o">moviegoers</span> by 10 <span class="kw kw-y">million</span>, and more than <span class="kw kw-g">half</span>
of which are young <span class="kw kw-c">people</span> and children. It is <span class="kw kw-b">planned</span> to open another <span class="kw kw-v">900</span> cinema centers <span class="kw kw-r">by</span> 2030,
cinema <span class="kw kw-o">halls</span>. It seems to <span class="kw kw-y">me</span> that this is the <span class="kw kw-g">most</span> important task <span class="kw kw-c">that</span> is being carried out
Government, Ministry of Culture.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">过去</span>十年
全国<span class="kw kw-o">各地</span>新开设了<span class="kw kw-y">超过</span> 15 个电影院。<span class="kw kw-g">每年</span>我们

<span class="kw kw-g">电影</span>院大厅。<span class="kw kw-c">在我</span>看来，这是<span class="kw kw-b">正在</span>执行的最重要的任务
政府、文化部。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 Но в <span class="kw kw-r">этом</span> смысле то <span class="kw kw-o">поручение</span>, которое Вы <span class="kw kw-y">дали</span> на прошлом Совете по <span class="kw kw-g">культуре</span>, – составить список <span class="kw kw-c">100</span>

<span class="kw kw-g">людей</span>, наших граждан, <span class="kw kw-c">возможностью</span> смотреть кино. <span class="kw kw-b">Хорошо</span> бы, чтобы <span class="kw kw-v">они</span> были

кино.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">But</span> in this sense, the <span class="kw kw-o">instruction</span> that you <span class="kw kw-y">gave</span> at the last <span class="kw kw-g">Council</span> on Culture was to compile a <span class="kw kw-c">list</span> of 100
the best <span class="kw kw-b">films</span> for mandatory screening in <span class="kw kw-v">educational</span> institutions, in my <span class="kw kw-r">opinion</span>, is even more <span class="kw kw-o">important</span>, because it <span class="kw kw-y">seems</span> to me that <span class="kw kw-g">it</span> is not enough to <span class="kw kw-c">provide</span>
people, our <span class="kw kw-b">citizens</span>, with the opportunity to watch movies. It would be nice if they were
prepared to truly be able to evaluate correctly
cinema.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">但从</span>这个意义<span class="kw kw-o">上说</span>，您在上届<span class="kw kw-y">文化</span>理事会上<span class="kw kw-g">给出</span>的指示是<span class="kw kw-c">编制</span>一份包含 100 <span class="kw kw-b">项的</span>清单。
在我<span class="kw kw-v">看来</span>，在教育机<span class="kw kw-r">构强</span>制放映的<span class="kw kw-o">最佳</span>影片更为<span class="kw kw-y">重要</span>，因为在我<span class="kw kw-g">看来</span>，提供这些<span class="kw kw-c">还不</span>够
人们，<span class="kw kw-b">我们</span>的公民，<span class="kw kw-v">有机</span>会观看电<span class="kw kw-r">影</span>。如果他们<span class="kw kw-o">是就</span>好了
准备好真正能够正确评估
电影院。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 И <span class="kw kw-r">этом</span> <span class="kw kw-o">смысле</span> <span class="kw kw-y">эта</span>
<span class="kw kw-g">инициатива</span> – <span class="kw kw-c">ввести</span> в <span class="kw kw-b">основные</span> учебные программы <span class="kw kw-v">предмет</span> «История отечественного
кино», <span class="kw kw-r">мне</span> кажется, очень важная, <span class="kw kw-o">очень</span> актуальная. <p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 And in <span class="kw kw-r">this</span> <span class="kw kw-o">sense</span> this

Education <span class="kw kw-c">approved</span> this list.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">从这</span>个意义上<span class="kw kw-o">说</span>
倡议 - 将“俄罗<span class="kw kw-y">斯史</span>”主题引入<span class="kw kw-g">主要</span>课程
电影”，<span class="kw kw-c">在我</span>看来非常<span class="kw kw-b">重要</span>，非常相关。<span class="kw kw-v">我们</span>准备了 100 <span class="kw kw-r">幅画</span>作的清单。<span class="kw kw-o">它得</span>到了文化<span class="kw kw-y">委员</span>会的批准，<span class="kw kw-g">并与</span>教育部和<span class="kw kw-c">克拉</span>夫佐夫部<span class="kw kw-b">长举</span>行了会议，<span class="kw kw-v">该部</span>还
教育部门批准了这份名单。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Должен</span> сказать,
выяснилось, что не <span class="kw kw-o">так</span> легко создать <span class="kw kw-y">такой</span> список. Казалось <span class="kw kw-g">бы</span>, чего легче?
<span class="kw kw-c">Бери</span> фильмы, которые <span class="kw kw-b">нравятся</span>! Но в этом и проблема, что <span class="kw kw-v">много</span> было списков,
<span class="kw kw-r">которые</span> были созданы по <span class="kw kw-o">субъективным</span> каким-то мотивам: <span class="kw kw-y">мне</span> понравилась картина,
я <span class="kw kw-g">видел</span> – давайте её <span class="kw kw-c">включим</span>. Но мне кажется, и <span class="kw kw-b">нам</span> показалось, что это не очень <span class="kw kw-v">верный</span> принцип.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 I <span class="kw kw-r">must</span> say
It <span class="kw kw-o">turned</span> out that <span class="kw kw-y">it</span> is not so <span class="kw kw-g">easy</span> to create such a <span class="kw kw-c">list</span>. It would <span class="kw kw-b">seem</span>, what is easier?
<span class="kw kw-v">Take</span> the films you <span class="kw kw-r">like</span>! But that’s the <span class="kw kw-o">problem</span>, there were a lot of <span class="kw kw-y">lists</span>,
which were created for <span class="kw kw-g">some</span> subjective reasons: I <span class="kw kw-c">liked</span> the picture,
I saw <span class="kw kw-b">it</span> - let&#x27;s <span class="kw kw-v">turn</span> it on. But <span class="kw kw-r">it</span> seems to me, and <span class="kw kw-o">it</span> seemed to us, <span class="kw kw-y">that</span> this is not a very correct principle.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">我必</span>须说
事实<span class="kw kw-o">证明</span>，创建这样<span class="kw kw-y">一个</span>列表并不<span class="kw kw-g">是那</span>么容易。<span class="kw kw-c">看起</span>来，还有<span class="kw kw-b">什么</span>更容易的<span class="kw kw-v">呢</span>？
喜欢的电<span class="kw kw-r">影就</span>拿去吧！<span class="kw kw-o">但这</span>就是问题<span class="kw kw-y">所在</span>，有很多列<span class="kw kw-g">表</span>，
这些是出<span class="kw kw-c">于一</span>些主观原<span class="kw kw-b">因而</span>创建的：<span class="kw kw-v">我喜</span>欢这张照<span class="kw kw-r">片</span>，
我看到了 - <span class="kw kw-o">让我</span>们打开它。<span class="kw kw-y">但在</span>我看来，<span class="kw kw-g">在我</span>们看来，这并不是一个非常正确的原则。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 Это <span class="kw kw-r">образовательная</span>
<span class="kw kw-o">программа</span> – образовательные программы <span class="kw kw-y">должны</span> основываться на изучении прежде
<span class="kw kw-g">всего</span> классических произведений. Наше <span class="kw kw-c">отечественное</span> кино уже имеет <span class="kw kw-b">набор</span>
произведений таких мастеров, <span class="kw kw-v">которых</span> можно считать классиками. <span class="kw kw-r">То</span> есть это то,
что проверено <span class="kw kw-o">временем</span>.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">This</span> is <span class="kw kw-o">educational</span>
program – educational <span class="kw kw-y">programs</span> should be based on learning <span class="kw kw-g">before</span>
total classical works. <span class="kw kw-c">Our</span> domestic cinema already <span class="kw kw-b">has</span> a set
works of such <span class="kw kw-v">masters</span> who can be considered <span class="kw kw-r">classics</span>. That is, this is what
<span class="kw kw-o">which</span> has stood the test of <span class="kw kw-y">time</span>.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">这是</span>有教育意<span class="kw kw-o">义的</span>
计划——教育<span class="kw kw-y">计划</span>应以之前<span class="kw kw-g">的学</span>习为基础
<span class="kw kw-c">经典</span>作品总量。<span class="kw kw-b">我们</span>国内的电<span class="kw kw-v">影院</span>已经有一<span class="kw kw-r">套了</span>
这些大师<span class="kw kw-o">的作</span>品都堪称<span class="kw kw-y">经典</span>。也就是说，<span class="kw kw-g">这就</span>是
经受住了时间的考验。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Мы</span> пошли по этому <span class="kw kw-o">пути</span>,
как, собственно, преподавание <span class="kw kw-y">художественной</span> литературы и других <span class="kw kw-g">предметов</span>, и подготовили, отобрали <span class="kw kw-c">50</span> режиссёров, которых <span class="kw kw-b">можно</span> считать классиками в <span class="kw kw-v">нашем</span>
кино, и взяли у <span class="kw kw-r">каждого</span> из них по две <span class="kw kw-o">картины</span> – у нас получилось <span class="kw kw-y">100</span> картин.
Теперь <span class="kw kw-g">задача</span>, чтобы эти <span class="kw kw-c">картины</span> действительно были… <span class="kw kw-b">Каким-то</span> образом
организовать <span class="kw kw-v">преподавание</span> в школах.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">We</span> went down <span class="kw kw-o">this</span> path
how, in <span class="kw kw-y">fact</span>, the teaching of fiction and <span class="kw kw-g">other</span> subjects, and prepared and <span class="kw kw-c">selected</span> 50 directors <span class="kw kw-b">who</span> can be considered <span class="kw kw-v">classics</span> in our
cinema, and <span class="kw kw-r">took</span> two pictures <span class="kw kw-o">from</span> each of them - <span class="kw kw-y">we</span> got 100 <span class="kw kw-g">pictures</span>.
Now the task is for <span class="kw kw-c">these</span> pictures to really be... <span class="kw kw-b">Somehow</span>
organize teaching in schools.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">我们</span>沿着这条<span class="kw kw-o">路走</span>下去
事实<span class="kw kw-y">上</span>，如何在小<span class="kw kw-g">说和</span>其他科目<span class="kw kw-c">的教</span>学中，准备<span class="kw kw-b">和挑</span>选出50位可<span class="kw kw-v">以被</span>视为我们<span class="kw kw-r">的经</span>典的导演
<span class="kw kw-o">电影</span>院，并为<span class="kw kw-y">他们</span>每人拍了<span class="kw kw-g">两张</span>照片——我们<span class="kw kw-c">得到</span>了 100 张照<span class="kw kw-b">片</span>。
现在的任<span class="kw kw-v">务是</span>让这些照<span class="kw kw-r">片真</span>正......以某种方式
组织学校教学。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Министерство</span> просвещения
на наших последних <span class="kw kw-o">встречах</span>, – это дело непростое, – но, во <span class="kw kw-y">всяком</span> случае, они
взялись за это. <span class="kw kw-g">Надеюсь</span>, что это будет реализовано, потому что <span class="kw kw-c">всё-таки</span>, мне
кажется, это важнейшая <span class="kw kw-b">сегодня</span> задача.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">Ministry</span> of Education

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Мне</span> хотелось бы <span class="kw kw-o">ещё</span> один

<div class="triad">

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">弗拉</span>基米尔·<span class="kw kw-o">弗拉</span>基米罗维<span class="kw kw-y">奇</span>，我们

<div class="triad">

<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">We</span> <span class="kw kw-o">ask</span> <span class="kw kw-y">yours</span>, <span class="kw kw-g">Vladimir</span>

tool. <span class="kw kw-b">This</span> could be seen, viewed, <span class="kw kw-v">assessed</span> during the start of the SVO,

工具。这可<span class="kw kw-b">以在</span> SVO 启动期间<span class="kw kw-v">看到</span>、观察和评<span class="kw kw-r">估</span>，

<div class="triad">

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Вот</span> уважаемая Татьяна <span class="kw kw-o">Алексеевна</span> Голикова – она <span class="kw kw-y">председатель</span> совета Фонда <span class="kw kw-g">кино</span>, и она заместитель <span class="kw kw-c">Председателя</span> Правительства. <span class="kw kw-v">Фонда</span> кино, на котором <span class="kw kw-r">рассматривается</span> вопрос о выделении <span class="kw kw-o">средств</span>, с учётом неоднократных <span class="kw kw-y">переносов</span> достигло более <span class="kw kw-g">месяца</span> в связи с высокой <span class="kw kw-c">профессиональной</span> занятостью руководства <span class="kw kw-b">совета</span> Фонда. Согласен. С <span class="kw kw-v">учётом</span> данных
задержек <span class="kw kw-r">доведение</span> средств

доведение средств <span class="kw kw-b">эквивалентно</span> потере производственного <span class="kw kw-v">года</span> на 90 процентов, <span class="kw kw-r">съёмочного</span> процесса, потому что <span class="kw kw-o">он</span> приходится как раз на <span class="kw kw-y">лето</span>. Если в феврале <span class="kw kw-g">мы</span> должны собраться <span class="kw kw-c">для</span> того, чтобы выяснить, кому, какой картине дать деньги, а потом это переносится на апрель, то уже в мае я снимать не смогу, я потерял год. Я потерял и время начала съёмок, и время
сдачи картины.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">Here</span> is dear Tatyana <span class="kw kw-o">Alekseevna</span> Golikova - she is the <span class="kw kw-y">chairman</span> of the board of the Cinema <span class="kw kw-g">Fund</span>, and she is the Deputy <span class="kw kw-c">Prime</span> Minister. Vladimirovich. What, <span class="kw kw-r">look</span>, is happening. It is <span class="kw kw-o">impossible</span> to subsidize a painting <span class="kw kw-y">without</span> a decision from the <span class="kw kw-g">Foundation</span>&#x27;s council.

Agree. Given the <span class="kw kw-y">data</span>
delays in bringing <span class="kw kw-g">funds</span>
government support for <span class="kw kw-c">film</span> companies was provided <span class="kw kw-b">only</span> in August and September. <span class="kw kw-v">That</span> is later
bringing in <span class="kw kw-r">funds</span> is equivalent to losing <span class="kw kw-o">90</span> percent of the production <span class="kw kw-y">year</span>, the filming process, <span class="kw kw-g">because</span> it falls <span class="kw kw-c">right</span> in the summer. If in <span class="kw kw-b">February</span> we have to <span class="kw kw-v">get</span> together to figure <span class="kw kw-r">out</span> who to give <span class="kw kw-o">money</span> to which film, and <span class="kw kw-y">then</span> this is postponed to <span class="kw kw-g">April</span>, then in May I <span class="kw kw-c">won</span>’t be able to shoot, I’<span class="kw kw-b">ve</span> lost a year. <p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">这是</span>亲爱的塔<span class="kw kw-o">季扬</span>娜·阿列<span class="kw kw-y">克谢</span>耶夫娜·<span class="kw kw-g">戈利</span>科娃——她是<span class="kw kw-c">电影</span>基金会董<span class="kw kw-b">事会</span>主席，也是<span class="kw kw-v">副总</span>理。她的<span class="kw kw-r">副手</span>是Molchanov Denis先生

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">今年</span> Soyuzmultfilm 正在制作

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 Но <span class="kw kw-r">остаётся</span> нерешённым вопрос, <span class="kw kw-o">касающийся</span> творческих мастерских и <span class="kw kw-y">тысяч</span> художников. Ведь

<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">But</span> the issue remains <span class="kw kw-o">unresolved</span> regarding creative <span class="kw kw-y">workshops</span> and thousands of artists. <span class="kw kw-g">After</span> all
Most <span class="kw kw-c">artists</span> cannot rent <span class="kw kw-b">space</span> at commercial <span class="kw kw-v">prices</span> and compete with business. <span class="kw kw-r">Historically</span>, since Soviet <span class="kw kw-o">times</span> and even

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">弗拉</span>基米尔·<span class="kw kw-o">普京</span>：安德烈·<span class="kw kw-y">尼古</span>拉耶维奇，

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 Я <span class="kw kw-r">вам</span> обещаю, что мы… Поручение – это <span class="kw kw-o">по-другому</span> должно звучать, это

<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 I <span class="kw kw-r">promise</span> <span class="kw kw-o">you</span> <span class="kw kw-y">that</span> <span class="kw kw-g">we</span>... The <span class="kw kw-c">order</span> - it <span class="kw kw-b">should</span> sound different, <span class="kw kw-v">it</span>

<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">我向</span><span class="kw kw-o">你保</span>证我们...<span class="kw kw-y">顺序</span> - 听起来应该不<span class="kw kw-g">同</span>，它

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Тоже</span> <span class="kw kw-o">попрошу</span> Администрацию, в <span class="kw kw-y">данном</span> случае опять <span class="kw kw-g">Владимира</span> Ростиславовича Мединского, <span class="kw kw-c">чтобы</span> он подготовил <span class="kw kw-b">вот</span> эти

<div class="triad">

<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 На <span class="kw kw-r">сегодняшний</span> день Большой <span class="kw kw-o">Московский</span> цирк, Российская <span class="kw kw-y">государственная</span> цирковая компания на <span class="kw kw-g">постоянной</span> основе работают в <span class="kw kw-c">наших</span> исторических регионах. С <span class="kw kw-b">2022</span> года мы
<span class="kw kw-v">представили</span> на Донбассе, а именно в <span class="kw kw-r">Луганске</span>, Донецке, Мариуполе, <span class="kw kw-o">Шахтёрске</span>, уже более 800 представлений, которые посетили более миллиона человек.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-en">🔹 <span class="kw kw-r">Today</span>, the <span class="kw kw-o">Great</span> <span class="kw kw-y">Moscow</span> Circus and the <span class="kw kw-g">Russian</span> State Circus Company <span class="kw kw-c">operate</span> on an ongoing basis in our <span class="kw kw-b">historical</span> regions. From 2022 <span class="kw kw-v">we</span>
presented in the Donbass, namely in <span class="kw kw-r">Lugansk</span>, Donetsk, Mariupol, Shakhtersk, <span class="kw kw-o">more</span> than 800 performances, <span class="kw kw-y">which</span> were attended by more <span class="kw kw-g">than</span> a million people.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">如今</span>，莫斯科大<span class="kw kw-o">马戏</span>团和俄罗<span class="kw kw-y">斯国</span>家马戏团<span class="kw kw-g">在我</span>们的历史<span class="kw kw-c">地区</span>持续运营。从2022<span class="kw kw-b">年起</span>我们
在顿<span class="kw kw-v">巴斯</span>，即卢甘斯<span class="kw kw-r">克</span>、顿涅茨克、<span class="kw kw-o">马里</span>乌波尔、<span class="kw kw-y">沙赫</span>特斯克进<span class="kw kw-g">行了</span>800多场演出，观看人数超过100万人。</p>
</div>

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 <span class="kw kw-r">Особенно</span>
<span class="kw kw-o">радует</span>, что <span class="kw kw-y">уже</span> в <span class="kw kw-g">этом</span> <span class="kw kw-c">году</span> Донецкий и Луганский цирк <span class="kw kw-b">станут</span> частью «Росгосцирка». There was a direct hit in the <span class="kw kw-y">Lugansk</span> circus. Circuses today are <span class="kw kw-g">experiencing</span> certain difficulties, but <span class="kw kw-c">we</span> support them.</p>
<p class="tri-line tri-zh">🔸 <span class="kw kw-r">尤其</span><span class="kw kw-o">是</span>

<div class="triad">

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 Я <span class="kw kw-r">знаю</span>, что мы находим

<div class="triad">
<p class="tri-line tri-ru">🔻 В.<span class="kw kw-r">Путин</span>: <span class="kw kw-o">Ольга</span> <span class="kw kw-y">Борисовна</span>, мне
<span class="kw kw-g">кажется</span>, надо поддержать. Там, <span class="kw kw-c">конечно</span>, не только тигры Эдгарда <span class="kw kw-b">Вальтеровича</span> бегают
и пугают зрителей, <span class="kw kw-v">восхищают</span>
зрителей
